 1
 akbar kii umr mahaj 13 saal thi jab unhone rajgaddi sanbhali thi
 2

 3

 Chidambaram said that under the auction process of market regulator Sebi, the current process of setting limits for companies to raise funds through bonds can be replaced by the process adopted in infrastructure (infra) bonds
 tippaniyan He said that the government bond limit would be increased whenever needed

 The Finance Minister said that investment rules have been simplified for Foreign Institutional Investors (fiis)
 unke liye sarkari pratibhutiyon or company kshetra ke rinpatron main nivesh niyamon ko udaar banaaya gaya he
 He said, with effect from April 1, 2013, FII investment would facilitate investment in only two broad categories instead of investment in the existing individual categories
 ek shrenee sarkari pratibhutiyon main nivesh kii hogi, jise 5 arab dollar badhaakar 25 arab dollar kar diya gaya he or duusari shrenee corporate bond kii hogi

 in donon vidhayakon se pehle congress apane vidhayak roshan beg ko party se nilambit kar chuki he
 Baig is busy praising BJP and Modi these days
 is tarah se congress ke vidhayakon kii sankhya lagaataar ghat rahi he

 is dauraan kuch anya vidhayakon ke istipha die jane ke sawaal par unhone kaha tha ki apni yojana ke bare main bataa nahin sakate

 'silent oparation lotus' ke jariye bijepi kaa makasad karnataka kii satta par kabiz hone kaa he
 For this, Congress and JDS mlas have to resign from the membership of the assembly
 sutron kii maane to is ranneeti ke tahat agle kuch dinon main congress-jedies ke har roj ek yaa do vidhayak apane pad se istipha denge taaki kumaraswami ke netritv vaali jedies-congress gathbandhan sarkaar ke vidhayakon kii sankhya ghatakar alpamat main aa jaae
 Explain that the number of congress-jds mlas in the Karnataka Legislative Assembly is continuously decreasing
 karnataka main kul 224 vidhansabha siten hai, bahumat ke liye 113 vidhayak chahie
 BJP currently has 105 mlas
 jabaki congress ke paas 80 or jedies ke paas 37 vidhayak hai
 Thus, both have a total of 117 mlas
 bispi or nirdaleey vidhayak bhi gathbandhan kaa samarthan kar rahe hai
 However, after the resignation of two Congress mlas and expulsion of one MLA, the number of Congress mlas has been reduced to 77
 congress-jedies kii sankhya 114 rah gai he
 At the same time, BJP is claiming that 6 Congress mlas and 2 JDS mlas are secretly supported, who will resign soon
 bijepi pradesh main sarkaar banane kii ummid lagaae baithi he or lagaataar iske liye daawey bhi kar rahi he
 The resignation of jds-congress mlas is increasing Kumaraswamy's troubles, but the BJP is not in a position to form a government
 yahi vajah he ki bijepi silent oparation lotus chalaa rahi he, taaki aisi sthiti bane jab kumaraswami bahumat se neeche aa jaaen or bijepi apni sarkaar banane kaa daawa pesh kare
 Significantly, through Operation Lotus, BJP was successful in forming the government in Karnataka in 2008 also
 us samay bijepi 224 main se 110 siten jitkar ai thi
 In such a situation, BJP used Operation Lotus to touch the majority figure
 congress or jedies ke aath vidhayakon ne vyaktigat kaarnon kaa hawala dete hue vidhansabha kii sadsyta se istipha de diya tha

 mahipalpur main sil hue 70 se zyada hotalon ke khulne kaa rasta saaf ho gaya he

 vaise is puri prakriya main 6 hafte lagenge
 Hotel owners will have to submit all the documents of terms, condition and sanction to the Delhi Pollution Control Committee in the next two weeks
 phir cameti haftebhar main gadabadiyaan bataaegi, or unhen dur karne ke liye do hafte kaa vaqt milegaa
 DPCC lawyer Sanjeev Rally said that the task of investigating whether the documents of these hotels are correct or not has been entrusted to the Delhi Pollution Control Committee
 or yahaan se anumati milane ke baad hi hotel chaalu ho paaenge
 The comments hotel maalikon ko dipisisi main jurmaana bhi bharna hoga
 Hotels with less than 25 rooms will have to pay Rs 1 lakh, hotels with 25 to 49 rooms and Rs 5 lakh for hotels with 50 or more rooms
 sari prakriya shuru karne ke pehle hafte bhar main sabhi sil hue hotel ko ek saal ke liye 5 lakh kaa secority band bharna hoga
